2b6(mdo): nags rnams dang / khrus kyi rdzong gi rnams dang / gser gyi tso mo rnams dang / 'bab chu dang / rin po che'i rang bzhin gyi rababargya rnams la blta ba sdug pa'i bya rnams kyis kun nas sgra 'dron pa dang

10b3(mdo): di tshon shin tu lhag par gyur ba'i nags tshal gyi phreng ba mdzes pa rnams mthong ba ni pa rnam par dgyes pa'i ba dU ts+tsha'i sngon shing mchog tu'abar 'arnams kyis nye bar mdzes pa dang / de bzhin du'ir/ 
10b4(mdo): la'i shi 'i tshogs rnams kyis nye bar mdzes par byas pa rnams kyis kyang ri tshogs rnam par mdzes par byed pa yinano// dashar yang lta de nyid kyis legs par mthong ba rnams rin po che 'dun / 
10b5(mdo): ma par bkra par byas pa pad pa 'dzing du rnams kyis nye bar mdzes pa'i dgas kyi rgyal po rnam par mdzes pa rnams so// dedag rnabs thams cad na yang rtag par thun mi 'argyad pa kur tu rtog pa rnam
10b6(mdo): byad rnams dang ldan pa dpe med par gzugs dang lang tshol bab cing rgyad dang byad rnams dang ldan pa'i lha dang lha mo'i tshogs brgya stong gis
11a1(mdo): songs sug sa sa ma pa yangs pa chags pa rnamasas lharnams 'ga' nag ni kun nas gnas te rtsom byed kyi skyon dang rnam par bral bar gyur pa'i rdzas kyi dadang dri da
11a2(mdo): rnams spyod par byed pa'i myos byed de dag rnams 'byung bar byed cing rgyags pa ladon ci 'i lhar gyig smad pa'i 'kho na po sa dang ban pa nas 'do/ rnam pa sna tshogs par gyur pa'i nag/

11a4(mdo): par bkra' rnams la 'tshe bag dang ldan pa'i lus can rnams rtse dga' bar byed do// lha gzhan dag rlabs kyang de khon bzhin du lhan cig spyod po rnams dang bcas pas rang dang gzhan rnams la yang
11a5(mdo): mchog tu dge' bar 'gyur ba'i ljin zhing gis rab gang pa'i nanam kyi phreng po mangs pa rnams la rol mo ma byed rnapas dang gang dang rdo sgra dang bcas pa'i rnardzas kyi 'dod pa'i phor tan ldarnams kyi
11a6(mdo): langs rnams da kyib ldan no// debazhin dun pa che bdun gyi rang bzhin gyi sngon shi shin da rnams dang ba rnams su song bar gyur nas de dzin bzhin du dka' ba byed

11b1(mdo): drim pa med pa'i 'bras bu'i sred pa rnams la rnam par chags pa'i yi kun rnams mthun pas snying kun tu rgyas par rje dga' bar byed pa'i 'dod pa rnams nyid kyis kyang ngoms pa med pa/ med pas rnam par
11b2(mdo): 'i yid can rnams sgolnga la rab tu rten par byed pa gang yin pa'i 'dod pa'i rtsa rnams su rab pa yin /  shin du na dgas ga dmas pa stan mas par byu 'i ba ma'i 'ad 'i rdzobs 'ad ma
11b3(mdo): logs par gnas par byasan pa myos byed zung 'a byed de/ 'odas myo byed kyi nyanye sar rnamam kyis kyang dun tugs par ni mi gyur // rnas pa da ga bya dang bdon rnams dpe med par gyur pa'i btur bdedang rnams kyis 'a len pa
11b4(mdo): gagasapas bsgos pa yin no// yang gzhand ga rnam ni 'chags pa' 'ab ba cu rnams kyi ngos gnyis su lnga de dag rnams pan drun du thog sa su gyung pas dpe med pa'i rdzas kyi bde la sa pa dum rnas nga la nye bar longs spyod par byed do// gzhan pa g+ha

14a1(mdo): rnams kyis kyang nye bar 'khor ba rnams nas yongs su bskor bar gyur pa'i mchor btu zhi ba'i spyod pas rgya ba rnams kyi gnas zhes bya ba'i dri'i khrod da gangs pa yin no//
